            data-uotrack="InlineShareCommentsBtn"><span class="inline-share-count inline-share-count-comments">

            </span><span class="inline-share-btn-label inline-share-btn-label-comments">COMMENT</span></span><span
        class="inline-share-btn inline-share-btn-email"
        data-share-method="email"
        data-uotrack="InlineShareEmailBtn"><span class="inline-share-count inline-share-count-email"></span><span class="inline-share-btn-label inline-share-btn-label-email">EMAIL</span></span><span
         class="inline-share-btn inline-share-btn-more"
         data-share-method="facebook"
         data-uotrack="InlineShareMoreBtn"><span class="inline-share-count inline-share-count-more"></span><span class="inline-share-btn-label inline-share-btn-label-more">MORE</span></span></div></div><p>A defiant Cam Newton addressed reporters for the first time since the Carolina Panthers’ MVP quarterback walked out of news conference minutes after his team fell to the Denver Broncos at Super Bowl 50 on Sunday.</p><p>“I’ve been on the record saying that I’m a sore loser,"  Newton told reporters at the team’s practice facility in Charlotte on Tuesday. "Who likes to lose? You show me a good loser and I’m going to show you a loser. It’s not a popularity contest. I am here to win football games."</p><p>Added Newton: “I have said it since Day 1. I am who I am. I know what I’m capable of and I know where I am going. If you want me to conform, I’m not that guy. If you want me to be that type of person, I’m not that. I am happy to say that. This league is a great league with or without me. I understand that. I am my own person. I take pride in that.”</p><div id="module-position-O-zVq7knlvc" class="story-asset oembed-asset"><div class="story-oembed-wrap "><div 
        class="js-oembed story-oembed story-oembed-soundcloud story-oembed-type-rich"
        data-oembed-type="rich"
        data-oembed-provider="soundcloud"><iframe class="embedly-embed" src="//cdn.embedly.com/widgets/media.html?src=https%3A%2F%2Fw.soundcloud.com%2Fplayer%2F%3Fvisual%3Dtrue%26url%3Dhttp%253A%252F%252Fapi.soundcloud.com%252Ftracks%252F246036119%26show_artwork%3Dtrue&url=https%3A%2F%2Fsoundcloud.com%2Fnfljunkies%2Fdenver-broncos-dominant-defense-delivers-super-bowl-50-title&image=http%3A%2F%2Fi1.sndcdn.com%2Fartworks-000146354894-5dt769-t500x500.jpg&key=205dfc3e29a54717b61d110ab0ac5a3d&type=text%2Fhtml&schema=soundcloud" width="500" height="500" scrolling="no" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen></iframe></div></div></div><p>Newton was heavily criticized after he gave a handful of short answers to reporters and unexpectedly got up and exited the dais two minutes into the session. Newton was sacked seven times --- twice fumbling the ball, one of which was returned for a touchdown by the Broncos - and completed 18 of 41 passes for 265 yards. The Broncos won, 24-10.</p><p>"It happened," Newton said. "I didn’t want to talk to the media at the time. The truth of the matter is that I still don’t want to talk to the media."</p><div id="module-position-O-zVq7kTgtE" class="story-asset oembed-asset"><div class="story-oembed-wrap "><div 
        class="js-oembed story-oembed story-oembed-5min-video story-oembed-type-rich"
        data-oembed-type="rich"
        data-oembed-provider="5min-video"><iframe src="http://embed.5min.com/PlayerSeed/?sid=1789&width=100&height=auto&playList=519485049&responsive=true&ratio=1&align=1&pgType=console&pgTypeId=discovery-videoDetails-grabCodeBtn" style="margin: 0; border: 0;" width="600" height="350" marginHeight="0" marginWidth="0" scrolling="no" frameBorder="0"></iframe></div></div></div><p>Newton, who was selected as the league MVP on Saturday, gave some hope to Panthers fans.</p><p>“We will be back,” Newton said. “I mean that. We will be back.”</p><p><em>Follow A.J. Perez on Twitter <a href="http://www.twitter.com/byajperez">@byajperez</a>.</em></p><p><strong>PHOTOS: Best of Super Bowl 50</strong></p><div id="module-position-O-zVq7l5JvQ" class="story-asset gallery-asset"><div class="card-film inactive"></div><div class="sidebar-gallery-btn active"></div><div class="companion-story-gallery"><div class="gallery-sidebar-panel"><span class="gallery-sidebar-close"></span><div class="gallery-sidebar-toolbox share-pane social-pane "><span class="util-bar-flyout-nav-btn-wrap"><span
